<Pictures>None< /Pictures><Resp>None<//Resp>< Review>
I was very impressed. Cozy atmosphere and very kind staff. I ordered California roll with fried lobster. Was ordering a second of the same and waitress recommended the baked lobster. Both fried and grilled lobster were really good. Thankful for her recommendation as i enjoyed the baked lobster more than the fried and will be returning for more. I went there with my girlfriend and had a great time. Other couples were there so i would say this is good place to being a date.< /Review>

< review>
First time trying this new spot here locally in Eastvale. We came in around 7p.m. on a Sunday night. We were greeted right away. Staff was friendly and attentive. We sat at the sushi bar James was the chef. He took very good care of us. Everything was presented to us promptly after ordering. Being that the place was full of customers it was surprisingly quick for our orders. My over all experience was 5 stars. I'll definitely be back. Unfortunately no alcohol yet being that they are a new restaurant it takes time to process for the license. That was the only down side. But once that goes through they should be a nice addition to Eastvale.</review>

<Rating>5< /Rating><Gmap_id>0x80dccb27397d99fd:0x8603299b13164fe4</Gmap_id><Response>None< /Response>< Review>
First time trying this place and it was great! It's a nice spot for a quick lunch and what I like the most about this place is that you're not overwhelmed by the numerous options on the menu. I had the salmon crunch roll and tempura udon and it was delicious. The udon broth was flavorful and the noodles weren't too soft. The sushi was fresh and had an excellent rice/protein ratio. The staff was very kind and always had a smile when serving someone. Location wise, the parking can be tight since it's in a small shopping center but other than that, this place is a wonderful sushi spot.</Review>
